msg:This is the first bad review I have ever received in a hotel. From the first day I entered the hotel and took so much company, the waiter was too lazy to pay attention to you. Then when I checked in at the front desk, it took him more than half an hour to check in three rooms, and there was no one next to him. On the fourth day of our stay, we were called downstairs at 11 noon to ask if we needed to extend our room. Then we both said we wanted to extend our room. But when we came down to extend our room, they told us that there were only suites and no rooms. Moreover, I initially I paid 5,000 for pre-authorization and told them to extend our room without checking out. This kind of service is really very poor. You can consider several hotels nearby. Then the environment of the hotel is also bad, not as shown in the picture. good!
